主营产品：电镀标牌、金属铭牌、金属logo、五金铭牌、五金logo、热熔胶标牌、不锈钢腐蚀标牌、镭射logo、拉丝标牌、腐蚀标牌、镀金标牌、镀鉻标牌、不锈钢铭牌滴胶、不锈钢标牌、金属铭牌、胸牌、胸针、徽章、听筒网，喇叭网，弹片，装饰件等等。{"id":6182,"date":"2017-06-22T11:10:41","date_gmt":"2017-06-22T03:10:41","guid":{"rendered":"http:\/\/greater-bay.paper-com.com.hk\/?page_id=6182"},"modified":"2023-01-09T15:03:52","modified_gmt":"2023-01-09T07:03:52","slug":"exhibitors-link-preview","status":"publish","type":"page","link":"https:\/\/www.dmpshow.com\/exhibition-info\/exhibitors-link-preview\/","title":{"rendered":"\u5c55\u5546\u8fde\u7ed3\u53ca\u9884\u544a"},"content":{"rendered":"
